<ol start="2">
<li>Design an inverting amplifier with an input resistance of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>30</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">30\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">30</span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>  and a closed loop gain of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>10</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-10</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">10</span></span></span></span></span> .</li>
</ol>
<p>Given: Closed loop gain  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>10</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A_{CL}} = -10</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">CL</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">10</span></span></span></span></span>  and  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>30</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{R}_1 = 30\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">30</span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Formula: For Inverting amplifier, the closed loop gain  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A_{CL}} = -\mathrm{R}_i / \mathrm{R}_1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">CL</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Solution:  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex-error" title="ParseError: KaTeX parse error: Expected 'EOF', got '&amp;' at position 57: …\mathrm{R}_1 = &amp;̲gt; - (-10) \ti…" style="color: rgb(204, 0, 0);">\mathrm{R}_1 = -\mathrm{A}_{\mathrm{CL}} \mathrm{R}_1 = &amp;gt; - (-10) \times 30 \mathrm{K} \Omega = &amp;gt; 300 \mathrm{K} \Omega</span></span></p>
<ol start="3">
<li>An inverting amplifier has a load resistor of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>50</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">50\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">50</span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>  connected to its output. If the input voltage is  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0.5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0.5\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.5</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> , find the load current, output voltage and input current. Given:  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>20</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{1} = 20\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">20</span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span> ,  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mi>f</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>200</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{f} = 200\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">200</span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span> .</li>
</ol>
<p>Solution:</p>
<p>Input current  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>0.5</mn><mi>V</mi></mrow><mrow><mn>20</mn><mi>K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>0.025</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i = \frac{V_1}{R_1} = \frac{0.5V}{20K\Omega} = 0.025\mathrm{mA}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6595em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.3335em; vertical-align: -0.4451em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8884em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3173em;"><span style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.4101em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3173em;"><span style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4451em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2173em; vertical-align: -0.345em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8723em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">20</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord mtight">Ω</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.394em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0.5</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.345em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.025</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">mA</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Introduction to Operational Amplifiers</p>
<p>Output Voltage  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">i</mi><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0.025</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>200</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{0} = -\mathrm{i}R_{1} = -(0.025\times 200)\mathrm{V} = 5\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">i</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0.025</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">200</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Load current  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>V</mi><mi>G</mi></msub><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>5</mn><mi>V</mi></mrow><mrow><mn>50</mn><mi>K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>0.1</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I_{\mathrm{L}} = \frac{V_{G}}{R_{\mathrm{L}}} = \frac{5V}{50K\Omega} = 0.1\mathrm{mA}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.345em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8723em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">50</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord mtight">Ω</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.394em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">5</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.345em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.1</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">mA</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ol start="4">
<li>Find the output voltage of an OP-AMP inverting adder for the following sets of input voltages and resistors. <p>Solution:</p>

mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><mrow><mn>1</mn><mi>M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l} v _ {0} = - \left(K _ {1} V _ {1} + K _ {2} V _ {2} + K _ {3} V _ {3}\right) \\ K _ {1} = \frac {R _ {f}}{R _ {1}} = \frac {1 0 0 0 K \Omega}{2 5 0 K <p>Solution:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>v</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>R</mi><mi>f</mi></msub><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mfrac><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>v</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>−</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>R</mi><mi>f</mi></msub><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mfrac><msub><mi>v</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mfrac><mn>10</mn><mn>5</mn></mfrac><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mn>4</mn><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mn>10</mn><mn>5</mn></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>5</mn><mo>=</mo><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">v _ {0} = \left(1 + \frac {R _ {f}}{R _ {1}}\right) v _ {1} - \frac {R _ {f}}{R _ {1}} v _ {2} = \left(1 + \frac {1 0}{5}\right) 4 - \frac {1 0}{5} \times 5 = + 2 V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.95em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">(</span></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3214em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">5</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">10</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">)</span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.0074em; vertical-align: -0.686em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3214em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">5</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">10</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">+</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<ol start="6">
<li>A  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>5</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>mV</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>KHz</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">5 \, \text{mV}, 1 \, \text{KHz}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">mV</span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KHz</span></span></span></span></span></span>  sinusoidal signal is applied to the input of an OP-AMP integrator of Fig. 6.12(b) for which  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>100</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>K</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R = 100 \, \text{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">100</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">K</span></span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>  and  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi>μ</mi><mtext>F</mtext></mrow><annotation 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">μ</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">F</span></span></span></span></span></span> . Find the output voltage.</li>
</ol>
<p>Solution:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Scale&nbsp;factor</mtext><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>R</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><msup><mn>10</mn><mn>7</mn></msup><mo>×</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>6</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>10</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text {Scale factor} = - \frac {1}{C R} = \frac {1}{1 0 ^ {7} \times 1 0 ^ {- 6}} = - 1 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Scale&nbsp;factor</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.0074em; vertical-align: -0.686em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3214em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">CR</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.0908em; vertical-align: -0.7693em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3214em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7401em;"><span style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">7</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7401em;"><span style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">6</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7693em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">10</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>The equation for the sinusoidal voltage is</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>v</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>f</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">v _ {1} = 5 \sin 2 \pi f t = 5 \sin 2 0 0 0 \pi t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">sin</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6679em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">sin</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2000</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Obviously, it has been assumed that at  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6151em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> ,  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>v</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">v_1 = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>∴</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>10</mn><msubsup><mo>∫</mo><mn>0</mn><mi>t</mi></msubsup><mn>5</mn><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>50</mn><msub><mrow><mo fence="true">∣</mo><mfrac><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>cos</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow><mn>2000</mn></mfrac><mo fence="true">∣</mo></mrow><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mn>40</mn><mi>π</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>cos</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l} \therefore \quad V _ {0} (t) = - 1 0 \int_ {0} ^ {t} 5 \sin 2 0 0 0 \pi t = - 5 0 \left| \frac {- \cos 2 0 0 0 \pi t}{2 0 0 0} \right| _ {0} \\ = \frac {1}{4 0 \pi} (\cos 2 0 0 0 \pi t - 1) \\ \end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.5933em; vertical-align: -1.0466em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.5466em;"><span style="top: -3.5582em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel amsrm">∴</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="margin-right: 0.19445em; position: relative; top: -0.0006em;">∫</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9885em;"><span style="top: -2.3442em; margin-left: -0.1945em; <li>The input to the differentiator circuit of Fig. 6.14 is a sinusoidal voltage of peak value  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>5</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>mV</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">5 \, \text{mV}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">mV</span></span></span></span></span></span>  and frequency  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>KHz</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1 \, \text{KHz}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KHz</span></span></span></span></span></span> . Find out the output if  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>100</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>K</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R = 100 \, \text{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">100</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">K</span></span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>  and  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi>μ</mi><mtext>F</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C = 1 \, \mu\text{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">μ</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">F</span></span></span></span></span></span> .</li>

<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="solution">Solution:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#solution" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The equation of the input voltage is</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>v</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>π</mi><mo>×</mo><mn>1000</mn><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi><mtext> </mtext><mtext>mV</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">v_1 = 5 \sin 2\pi \times 1000t = 5 \sin 2000\pi t \, \text{mV}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7512em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">sin</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">sin</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2000</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">mV</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>scale factor =</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.25em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mtext>CR</mtext></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>=</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>6</mn></mrow></msup><mo>×</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mn>5</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0.1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><msub><mi>v</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>r</mi></mrow></msub></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0.1</mn><mfrac><mi>d</mi><mrow><mi>d</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>5</mn><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0.5</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>cos</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>cos</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mn>2000</mn><mi>π</mi><mi>t</mi><mtext> </mtext><mtext>mV</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
\text{CR} &amp;amp;= 10^{-6} \times 10^5 = 0.1 \\
v_{tr} &amp;amp;= 0.1 \frac{d}{dt} (5 \sin 2000\pi t) = (0.5 \times 2000\pi) \cos 2000\pi t \\
&amp;amp;= 1000\pi \cos 2000\pi t \, \text{mV}
\end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.3815em; vertical-align: -2.4408em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">mV</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.4408em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>As seen, output is a cosinusoidal voltage of frequency <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mtext> </mtext><mtext>KHz</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1 \, \text{KHz}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KHz</span></span></span></span></span></span> and peak value <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1000</mn><mi>π</mi><mtext> </mtext><mtext>mV</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1000\pi \, \text{mV}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">mV</span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Introduction to Operational Amplifiers</p>

<li>
<p>Common Mode Gain <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathrm{A}_{\mathrm{CM}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">CM</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> of an OP-AMP is ______

<li>
<p>CMRR =
(a) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A_d} / -\mathrm{A_{CM}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; (b) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A_d} / \mathrm{A_{CM}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">d</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">CM</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>

(d) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A_{CM}} / -\mathrm{A_d}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; </li>
<li>
<p>Ideal OP-AMP has ______
(a) Zero open loop gain
(b) Infinite open loop gain
(c) Positive open loop gain
(d) Negative open loop gain</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<ol start="23">
<li>OP-AMP need ______ for operation</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) One battery supply</p>
<p>(b) Dual battery supply</p>
<p>(c) Three phase supply</p>
<p>(d) Power supply</p>
<ol start="24">
<li>Lissajous figures are used for ______</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) determining an unknown frequency by comparing it with a known frequency.</p>
<p>(b) checking audio oscillator with a known frequency signal.</p>
<p>(c) checking audio amplifiers and feedback networks for phase shift.</p>
<p>(d) all the above.</p>
<ol start="25">
<li>The product of C and R in differentiator circuit is called ______</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) CR product of differentiator</p>
<p>(b) Time constant of differentiator</p>
<p>(c) Differentiation coefficient</p>
<p>(d) None of These</p>

<li>For the circuit shown in following figure, determine the output voltage.</li>
